msg:Let me first say the conclusion: the hotel hardware is worth the price, but remember not to book a price with meals included, otherwise you will feel that it has no cost-effectiveness.
1. Advantages. It has its own swimming pool and beach, and the price without meals is very cost-effective.
2. Disadvantages. It is said that dinner is until 10 o'clock, and if you go there at 9:30, it is basically leftovers, and no extra food will be given. Children will be charged according to their requirements, but please note my wording. During the Spring Festival, after 9:30, it is "leftovers", which cannot be eaten.
In short, the hotel can be stayed, but remember not to book a price with meals included.

msg:The hotel is located at the junction of Chengmai County and Haikou City. Although the hardware facilities are slightly old, it is still a luxury hotel. The front desk was upgraded to a room type with a terrace, which was a pleasant surprise. The hotel has its own beach with a nice view. In addition to the hot spring pool on the balcony of the room, there are also several public hot spring pools, which are open from 7:30 in the morning to 22:00. There is a shared motorcycle at the door, you can ride to the old market in Chengmai County to solve the catering problem, about 7 kilometers. A taxi from the hotel to Qilou Old Street is about 50 yuan. The hotel has a cdf free shuttle.
